6. Seed 文件占位资源策略
如果你希望 demo 模式更稳定，建议加一条规则：
策略
所有 seed 数据里的
image_url
可以先指向前端
public/placeholder-*.png
local_file_path
可以保留固定占位路径
当真实 provider 运行后，再用真实路径覆盖
推荐目录
frontend/public/
├─ placeholder-character.png
├─ placeholder-outfit.png
└─ placeholder-result.png
这意味着：
前端 demo 稳定可显示
后端 seed 不需要一开始就真的生成图片文件
真图生成后自然覆盖真实结果流

1.1 新增
frontend/src/store/refresh.store.ts
import { create } from "zustand";
interface RefreshState {
tasksTick: number;
resultsTick: number;
logsTick: number;
triggerTasksRefresh: () => void;
triggerResultsRefresh: () => void;
triggerLogsRefresh: () => void;
}
export const useRefreshStore = create<RefreshState>((set) => ({
tasksTick: 0,
resultsTick: 0,
logsTick: 0,
triggerTasksRefresh: () => set((s) => ({ tasksTick: s.tasksTick + 1 })),
triggerResultsRefresh: () => set((s) => ({ resultsTick: s.resultsTick + 1 })),
triggerLogsRefresh: () => set((s) => ({ logsTick: s.logsTick + 1 })),
}));
1.2 新增
frontend/src/hooks/use-polling.ts
"use client";
import { useEffect } from "react";
export function usePolling(callback: () => void | Promise<void>, intervalMs: number, enabled: boolean = true) {
useEffect(() => {
if (!enabled) return;
void callback();
const timer = setInterval(() => {
void callback();
}, intervalMs);
return () => clearInterval(timer);
}, [callback, intervalMs, enabled]);
}
1.3 修改
frontend/src/hooks/use-logs.ts
"use client";
import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { getTasks } from "@/services/api/task.api";
import { getExports } from "@/services/api/export.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useRefreshStore } from "@/store/refresh.store";
export function useLogs() {
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const logsTick = useRefreshStore((s) => s.logsTick);
const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [exportsList, setExportsList] = useState<any[]>([]);
const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const [taskRes, exportRes]: any = await Promise.all([
getTasks({ page: 1, pageSize: 20 }),
getExports(),
]);
setTasks(taskRes.data.items || []);
setExportsList(exportRes.data.items || []);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load logs";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
}, [setGlobalError, setGlobalLoading]);
1.4 修改
frontend/src/hooks/use-review.ts
"use client";
import { useCallback, useEffect } from "react";
import { getResults } from "@/services/api/result.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useResultStore } from "@/store/result.store";
import { useReviewStore } from "@/store/review.store";
import { useRefreshStore } from "@/store/refresh.store";
export function useReview() {
const selectedResultId = useReviewStore((s) => s.selectedResultId);
const selectResult = useReviewStore((s) => s.selectResult);
const items = useResultStore((s) => s.items);
const setItems = useResultStore((s) => s.setItems);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const resultsTick = useRefreshStore((s) => s.resultsTick);
const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const response = await getResults();
const nextItems = response.data.items;
setItems(nextItems);
if (!selectedResultId && nextItems.length > 0) {
selectResult(nextItems[0].id);
}
} catch (error) {
const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Failed to load results";
setGlobalError(message);
2. 前端：Result Detail 页面
现在有 Task Detail，但 Result 还缺一个真正的详情页。
2.1 修改
frontend/src/services/api/result.api.ts
import { apiRequest } from "./client";
import { ApiResponse, ListResponse } from "@/types/common";
import { GeneratedResult } from "@/types/result";
export function getResults(params?: {
status?: string;
characterId?: string;
outfitTemplateId?: string;
page?: number;
pageSize?: number;
}) {
const query = new URLSearchParams();
if (params?.status) query.set("status", params.status);
if (params?.characterId) query.set("character_id", params.characterId);
if (params?.outfitTemplateId) query.set("outfit_template_id", params.outfitTemplateId);
if (params?.page) query.set("page", String(params.page));
if (params?.pageSize) query.set("page_size", String(params.pageSize));
const suffix = query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : "";
return apiRequest<ApiResponse<ListResponse<GeneratedResult>>>(`/results${suffix}`);
}
export function getResultById(resultId: string) {
return apiRequest<ApiResponse<GeneratedResult>>(`/results/${resultId}`);
}

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useParams } from "next/navigation";

getResultById(id).then((res: any) => setResult(res.data));

return <div className="text-sm text-zinc-500">Loading result...</div>;
}
return (
<div className="space-y-6">

<img src={result.imageUrl || result.image_url} alt={result.id} className="w-full rounded-2xl object-cover" />

"use client";
interface DetailDrawerProps {
open: boolean;
title: string;
onClose: () => void;
children: React.ReactNode;
}
export function DetailDrawer({ open, title, onClose, children }: DetailDrawerProps) {
if (!open) return null;
return (
<div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex justify-end bg-black/50">
<div className="h-full w-full max-w-xl overflow-y-auto border-l border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950 p-6 shadow-2xl">
<div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between">
<h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">{title}</h2>
<button onClick={onClose} className="rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 px-3 py-1 text-sm text-zinc-100">
Close
</button>
</div>
{children}
</div>
</div>
);
}
4. 前端：Logs 分页骨架
4.1 修改
frontend/src/hooks/use-logs.ts
"use client";
import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { getTasks } from "@/services/api/task.api";
import { getExports } from "@/services/api/export.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
export function useLogs() {
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [exportsList, setExportsList] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [taskPage, setTaskPage] = useState(1);
const [taskPageSize] = useState(20);
const [taskTotal, setTaskTotal] = useState(0);
const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const [taskRes, exportRes]: any = await Promise.all([
getTasks({ page: taskPage, pageSize: taskPageSize }),
getExports(),
]);
setTasks(taskRes.data.items || []);
setTaskTotal(taskRes.data.pagination?.total || 0);
setExportsList(exportRes.data.items || []);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load logs";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
4.2 修改
frontend/src/app/logs/page.tsx
"use client";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/common/page-header";
import { AsyncState } from "@/components/common/async-state";
import { PaginationBar } from "@/components/common/pagination-bar";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useLogs } from "@/hooks/use-logs";
export default function LogsPage() {
const globalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.globalLoading);
const globalError = useAppStore((s) => s.globalError);
const { tasks, exportsList, taskPage, setTaskPage, taskPageSize, taskTotal } = useLogs();
return (
<div className="space-y-6">
<PageHeader title="Logs" description="Task and export activity overview." />
<AsyncState
loading={globalLoading}
error={globalError}
isEmpty={!tasks.length && !exportsList.length}
emptyTitle="No logs yet"
emptyDescription="Run some tasks or exports to populate activity logs."
>
<div className="grid gap-6 xl:grid-cols-2">
<div className="space-y-4 rounded-3xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950/70 p-4">
<h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Recent Tasks</h3>
<div className="space-y-3">
{tasks.map((task) => (
<div key={task.id} className="rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/70 p-3">
<div className="text-sm font-medium text-white">{task.id}</div>
<div className="text-xs text-zinc-400">{task.type} · {task.status}</div>
{task.error_message ? <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-rose-300">{task.error_message}</div> : null}
</div>
))}
</div>
<PaginationBar
page={taskPage}
pageSize={taskPageSize}
total={taskTotal}
onPrev={() => setTaskPage((p) => Math.max(1, p - 1))}
onNext={() => setTaskPage((p) => p + 1)}
/>
</div>
<div className="rounded-3xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950/70 p-4">
<h3 className="mb-4 text-lg font-semibold text-white">Recent Exports</h3>
<div className="space-y-3">
{exportsList.map((item) => (
<div key={item.id} className="rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/70 p-3">
<div className="text-sm font-medium text-white">{item.export_file_name}</div>
<div className="text-xs text-zinc-400">{item.status}</div>
</div>
))}
</div>
</div>
</div>
</AsyncState>
</div>
);
}

total,
} = useResults();

setDrawerOpen(true);
}

frontend/src/components/edit-studio/mask-list-panel.tsx
"use client";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { getMasks, MaskTemplate } from "@/services/api/mask.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useTaskStore } from "@/store/task.store";
import { MaskDetailDrawer } from "./mask-detail-drawer";
export function MaskListPanel() {
const pushToast = useAppStore((s) => s.pushToast);
const draft = useTaskStore((s) => s.draft);
const setDraft = useTaskStore((s) => s.setDraft);
const [items, setItems] = useState<MaskTemplate[]>([]);
const [drawerOpen, setDrawerOpen] = useState(false);
const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<any | null>(null);
useEffect(() => {
getMasks()
.then((res) => setItems(res.data.items))
.catch((e) => {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load masks";
pushToast({
type: "error",
title: "Mask load failed",
description: msg,
});
});
}, [pushToast]);
return (
<>
<div className="space-y-4 rounded-3xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950/70 p-4">
<h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Mask Templates</h3>
{!items.length ? (
<div className="text-sm text-zinc-500">No masks uploaded yet.</div>
) : (
<div className="grid gap-3">
{items.map((item) => (
<label
key={item.id}
className="flex cursor-pointer items-center gap-4 rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/70 p-3"
>
<input
type="radio"
name="maskTemplate"
checked={draft.maskTemplateId === item.id}
onChange={() => setDraft({ maskTemplateId: item.id })}
/>
<button type="button" onClick={() => { setSelectedItem(item); setDrawerOpen(true); }}>
<img src={item.image_url} className="h-16 w-16 rounded-xl object-cover" />
</button>
<div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
<div className="text-sm font-medium text-white">{item.name}</div>
<div className="text-xs text-zinc-500">{item.target_part}</div>
<div className="text-xs text-zinc-400">{item.code}</div>
</div>
</label>
))}
</div>
)}
</div>
<MaskDetailDrawer open={drawerOpen} item={selectedItem} onClose={() => setDrawerOpen(false)} />
</>
);
}

5. 前端：Export 历史分页骨架
5.1 修改
frontend/src/services/api/export.api.ts
export function getExports(params?: { page?: number; pageSize?: number }) {
const query = new URLSearchParams();
if (params?.page) query.set("page", String(params.page));
if (params?.pageSize) query.set("page_size", String(params.pageSize));
const suffix = query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : "";
return apiRequest(`/exports${suffix}`);
}

6. 批量 Rework / 批量 Promote 方案
这一批先给实施方案，不在这一轮里把所有代码铺满，避免改动过大。

: [
"result_1"
,
"result_2"
]
}
服务层：
循环调用
promote_result_to_base(result_id)
每个角色仅保留一个 main base
建议这部分留到 Batch 15 再展开完整代码。
7. 日志事件模型建议
当前 Logs 只是：
tasks
exports
建议下一步新增统一事件仓：
event_logs
├─ id
├─ created_at
├─ event_type
├─ actor
├─ target_type
├─ target_id
├─ summary
└─ metadata
可记录事件
task_created
task_failed
result_approved
result_reworked
result_promoted_to_base
export_created
mask_uploaded
这样 Logs 页面会更像真正的审计台。
8. 字段命名统一清理方案
这是当前工程后面非常值得做的一次“整理手术”。
当前问题
前后端混用了：
camelCase
snake_case
例如：
前端：
characterId
后端：
character_id
推荐方案
方案 A：前端 camelCase，后端 snake_case
API 层做映射转换
UI 与 Python 各自保持自然风格
方案 B：全部改 snake_case
更省事，但前端可读性略差
推荐
用
方案 A
：
前端 types / store / components 保持 camelCase
后端 schemas / services / repos 保持 snake_case
services/api/serializers.ts
做映射
建议新增文件
frontend/src/services/api/serializers.ts
提供：
toApiTaskPayload()
fromApiResult()
fromApiCharacter()
fromApiOutfit()
这块建议在 Batch 15 正式铺。

export function fromApiResult(input: any) {

1.2 修改
frontend/src/hooks/use-generate-task.ts
"use client";
import { createTask } from "@/services/api/task.api";
import { toApiTaskPayload } from "@/services/api/serializers";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useTaskStore } from "@/store/task.store";
export function useGenerateTask() {
const draft = useTaskStore((s) => s.draft);
const resetDraft = useTaskStore((s) => s.resetDraft);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const pushToast = useAppStore((s) => s.pushToast);
async function submitTask() {
try {
if (!draft.characterId) {
pushToast({
type: "error",
title: "Character required",
description: "Please select a character before submitting a task.",
});
return null;
}
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const response: any = await createTask(toApiTaskPayload(draft));
pushToast({
type: "success",
title: "Task created",
description: `Task ${response.data.id} created successfully.`,
});

5. 前端：Logs 页面切事件流
5.1 新增
frontend/src/services/api/event.api.ts
import { apiRequest } from "./client";
export function getEvents(params?: { eventType?: string; page?: number; pageSize?: number }) {
const query = new URLSearchParams();
if (params?.eventType) query.set("event_type", params.eventType);
if (params?.page) query.set("page", String(params.page));
if (params?.pageSize) query.set("page_size", String(params.pageSize));
const suffix = query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : "";
return apiRequest(`/events${suffix}`);
}
5.2 修改
frontend/src/hooks/use-logs.ts
"use client";
import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { getEvents } from "@/services/api/event.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
export function useLogs() {
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const [items, setItems] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
const [pageSize] = useState(20);
const [total, setTotal] = useState(0);
const [eventType, setEventType] = useState("");
const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const res: any = await getEvents({ eventType, page, pageSize });
setItems(res.data.items || []);
setTotal(res.data.pagination?.total || 0);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load logs";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
}, [eventType, page, pageSize, setGlobalError, setGlobalLoading]);
useEffect(() => {
void refresh();
}, [refresh]);

import { apiRequest } from "./client";
import { ApiResponse } from "@/types/common";
import { ReviewDecision, ReviewStatus } from "@/types/review";
export interface ReviewSubmitInput {
resultId: string;
status: ReviewStatus;
score: {
identityStability: number;
handIntegrity: number;
outfitReadability: number;
weaponCompleteness: number;
commercialReadiness: number;
};
comment?: string;
sendBackToEdit?: boolean;
}
export function submitReview(payload: ReviewSubmitInput) {
return apiRequest<ApiResponse<ReviewDecision>>("/reviews", {
method: "POST",
body: JSON.stringify(payload),
});
}
export function getReviews() {
return apiRequest("/reviews");
}

"use client";
import { submitBatchApprove, submitBatchRework, promoteBatchResults } from "@/services/api/review.api";
import { useResultStore } from "@/store/result.store";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
import { useReview } from "@/hooks/use-review";
import { useReviewBatchStore } from "@/store/review-batch.store";
export function ReviewBatchActions() {
const items = useResultStore((s) => s.items);
const pushToast = useAppStore((s) => s.pushToast);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const { refresh } = useReview();
const selectedResultIds = useReviewBatchStore((s) => s.selectedResultIds);
const selectAll = useReviewBatchStore((s) => s.selectAll);
const clear = useReviewBatchStore((s) => s.clear);
async function handleBatchApprove() {
if (!selectedResultIds.length) {
pushToast({
type: "info",
title: "Nothing selected",
description: "Select review results first.",
});
return;
}
try {
setGlobalLoading(true);
await submitBatchApprove(selectedResultIds);
pushToast({
type: "success",
title: "Batch approve complete",
description: `${selectedResultIds.length} results approved.`,
});
clear();

import { apiRequest } from "./client";
export function getTaskTrace(taskId: string) {
return apiRequest(`/traces/tasks/${taskId}`);
}
export function getResultTrace(resultId: string) {
return apiRequest(`/traces/results/${resultId}`);
}

2. 前端：Review History / Export History 接 AsyncState
2.1 修改
frontend/src/app/review/history/page.tsx
"use client";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/common/page-header";
import { AsyncState } from "@/components/common/async-state";
import { getReviews } from "@/services/api/review.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
export default function ReviewHistoryPage() {
const globalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.globalLoading);
const globalError = useAppStore((s) => s.globalError);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const [items, setItems] = useState<any[]>([]);
useEffect(() => {
async function run() {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const res: any = await getReviews();
setItems(res.data.items || []);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load review history";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
}
void run();
}, [setGlobalError, setGlobalLoading]);
return (
<div className="space-y-6">
<PageHeader title="Review History" description="Review decisions over time." />
2.2 修改
frontend/src/app/export/history/page.tsx
"use client";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/common/page-header";
import { PaginationBar } from "@/components/common/pagination-bar";
import { AsyncState } from "@/components/common/async-state";
import { getExports } from "@/services/api/export.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
export default function ExportHistoryPage() {
const globalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.globalLoading);
const globalError = useAppStore((s) => s.globalError);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const [items, setItems] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
const [pageSize] = useState(20);
const [total, setTotal] = useState(0);
useEffect(() => {
async function run() {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const res: any = await getExports({ page, pageSize });
setItems(res.data.items || []);
setTotal(res.data.pagination?.total || 0);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load export history";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
}

1.1 新增
frontend/src/components/logs/event-link.tsx
"use client";
import Link from "next/link";
interface EventLinkProps {
targetType?: string;
targetId?: string;
}
function resolveHref(targetType?: string, targetId?: string) {
if (!targetType || !targetId) return null;
switch (targetType) {
case "task":
return `/tasks/${targetId}`;
case "result":
return `/results/${targetId}`;
case "export":
return `/export/history`;
case "mask":
return `/edit-studio`;
default:
return null;
}
}
export function EventLink({ targetType, targetId }: EventLinkProps) {
const href = resolveHref(targetType, targetId);
if (!href) {
return <span className="text-xs text-zinc-500">No linked page</span>;
}
return (
<Link href={href} className="text-xs text-zinc-300 underline underline-offset-2 hover:text-white">
Open linked page

import { apiRequest } from "./client";
if (params?.outfitTemplateId) query.set("outfit_template_id", params.outfitTemplateId);
if (params?.page) query.set("page", String(params.page));
if (params?.pageSize) query.set("page_size", String(params.pageSize));
const suffix = query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : "";
const res = await apiRequest<ApiResponse<ListResponse<any>>>(`/results${suffix}`);
return {
...res,
data: {
...res.data,
items: (res.data.items || []).map(fromApiResult),
},
} as ApiResponse<ListResponse<GeneratedResult>>;
}
export async function getResultById(resultId: string) {
const res = await apiRequest<ApiResponse<any>>(`/results/${resultId}`);
return {
...res,
data: fromApiResult(res.data),
} as ApiResponse<GeneratedResult>;
}

import { apiRequest } from "./client";
import { fromApiCharacter } from "./serializers";
import { ApiResponse, ListResponse } from "@/types/common";
export interface BaseImageVersion {
id: string;
characterId: string;
version: string;
imageUrl: string;
thumbnailUrl?: string | null;
localFilePath?: string | null;
isMainBase: boolean;
sourceTaskId?: string | null;
sourcePrompt?: string | null;
notes?: string | null;
createdAt: string;
updatedAt: string;
}
function fromApiBaseImage(input: any): BaseImageVersion {
return {
id: input.id,
characterId: input.character_id,
version: input.version,
imageUrl: input.image_url,
thumbnailUrl: input.thumbnail_url,
localFilePath: input.local_file_path,
isMainBase: input.is_main_base,
sourceTaskId: input.source_task_id,
sourcePrompt: input.source_prompt,
notes: input.notes,
createdAt: input.created_at,
updatedAt: input.updated_at,
};
}
2.3 修改
frontend/src/services/api/outfit.api.ts
import { apiRequest } from "./client";
import { fromApiOutfit } from "./serializers";
import { ApiResponse, ListResponse } from "@/types/common";
export async function getOutfits(params?: {
keyword?: string;
theme?: string;
status?: string;
page?: number;
pageSize?: number;
}) {
const query = new URLSearchParams();
if (params?.keyword) query.set("keyword", params.keyword);
if (params?.theme) query.set("theme", params.theme);
if (params?.status) query.set("status", params.status);
if (params?.page) query.set("page", String(params.page));
if (params?.pageSize) query.set("page_size", String(params.pageSize));
const suffix = query.toString() ? `?${query.toString()}` : "";
const res = await apiRequest<ApiResponse<ListResponse<any>>>(`/outfits${suffix}`);
return {
...res,
data: {
...res.data,
items: (res.data.items || []).map(fromApiOutfit),
},
};
}

"use client";
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/common/page-header";
import { PaginationBar } from "@/components/common/pagination-bar";
import { AsyncState } from "@/components/common/async-state";
import { getExports } from "@/services/api/export.api";
import { useAppStore } from "@/store/app.store";
export default function ExportHistoryPage() {
const globalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.globalLoading);
const globalError = useAppStore((s) => s.globalError);
const setGlobalLoading = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalLoading);
const setGlobalError = useAppStore((s) => s.setGlobalError);
const [items, setItems] = useState<any[]>([]);
const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
const [pageSize] = useState(20);
const [total, setTotal] = useState(0);
const [keyword, setKeyword] = useState("");
useEffect(() => {
async function run() {
try {
setGlobalError(null);
setGlobalLoading(true);
const res: any = await getExports({ page, pageSize });
setItems(res.data.items || []);
setTotal(res.data.pagination?.total || 0);
} catch (e) {
const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Failed to load export history";
setGlobalError(msg);
} finally {
setGlobalLoading(false);
}
}
